2|18|SUMMUN BUKMUN ‘UMJUN FEHUM LA JERXHI’UNE

2|28|KEJFE TEKFURUNE BILLAHI WE KUNTUM ‘EMWATÆN FE’EHJAKUM THUMME JUMITUKUM THUMME JUHJIKUM THUMME ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE

2|102|WE ETTEBA’U MA TETLU ESH-SHEJATINU ‘ALA MULKI SULEJMANE WE MA KEFERE SULEJMANU WE LEKINNE ESH-SHEJATINE KEFERU JU’ALLIMUNE EN-NASE ES-SIHRE WE MA ‘UNZILE ‘ALEL-MELEKEJNI BIBABILE HARUTE WE MARUTE WE MA JU’ALLIMANI MIN ‘EHEDIN HETTA JEKULA ‘INNEMA NEHNU FI
2|103|WE LEW ‘ENNEHUM ‘AMENU WE ETTEKAW LEMETHUBETUN MIN ‘INDI ELLAHI HAJRUN LEW KANU JA’LEMUNE

11|23|‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI WE ‘EHBETU ‘ILA RABBIHIM ‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABUL-XHENNETI HUM FIHA HALIDUNE
11|24|METHELUL-FERIKAJNI KAL’A’MA WEL-’ESEMMI WEL-BESIRI WE ES-SEMI’I HEL JESTEWIJANI METHELÆN ‘EFELA TEDHEKKERUNE
11|25|WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA NUHÆN ‘ILA KAWMIHI ‘INNI LEKUM NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
11|26|‘EN LA TA’BUDU ‘ILLALLAHE ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘ALEJKUM ‘ADHABE JEWMIN ‘ELIMIN
11|27|FEKALEL-MELE’UL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN KAWMIHI MA NERAKE ‘ILLA BESHERÆN MITHLENA WE MA NERAKE ETTEBE’AKE ‘ILLAL-LEDHINE HUM ‘ERADHILUNA BADIJE ER-RE’JI WE MA NERA LEKUM ‘ALEJNA MIN FEDLIN BEL NEDHUNNUKUM KADHIBINE
11|28|KALE JA KAWMI ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN KUNTU ‘ALA BEJJINETIN MIN RABBI WE ‘ATANI REHMETEN MIN ‘INDIHI FA’UMMIJET ‘ALEJKUM ‘ENULZIMUKUMUHA WE ‘ENTUM LEHA KARIHUNE
11|29|WE JAKAWMI LA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MALÆN ‘IN ‘EXHRIJE ‘ILLA ‘ALA ELLAHI WE MA ‘ENA BITARIDIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘INNEHUM MULAKU RABBIHIM WE LEKINNI ‘ERAKUM KAWMÆN TEXHHELUNE
11|30|WE JAKAWMI MEN JENSURUNI MINEL-LAHI ‘IN TEREDTUHUM ‘EFELA TEDHEKKERUNE
11|31|WE LA ‘EKULU LEKUM ‘INDI HAZA’INU ELLAHI WE LA ‘A’LEMUL-GAJBE WE LA ‘EKULU ‘INNI MELEKUN WE LA ‘EKULU LILLEDHINE TEZDERI ‘A’JUNUKUM LEN JU’UTIJEHUMU ELLAHU HAJRÆN ELLAHU ‘A’LEMU BIMA FI ‘ENFUSIHIM ‘INNI ‘IDHÆN LEMINE EDH-DHALIMINE
11|32|KALU JA NUHU KAD XHADELTENA FE’EKTHERTE XHIDALENA FE’TINA BIMA TA’IDUNA ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
11|33|KALE ‘INNEMA JE’TIKUM BIHI ELLAHU ‘IN SHA’E WE MA ‘ENTUM BIMU’XHIZINE
11|34|WE LA JENFA’UKUM NUSHI ‘IN ‘EREDTU ‘EN ‘ENSEHE LEKUM ‘IN KANEL-LAHU JURIDU ‘EN JUGWIJEKUM HUWE REBBUKUM WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
11|35|‘EM JEKULUNE EFTERAHU KUL ‘INI EFTEREJTUHU FE’ALEJJE ‘IXHRAMI WE ‘ENA BERI’UN MIMMA TUXHRIMUNE
11|36|WE ‘UHIJE ‘ILA NUHIN ‘ENNEHU LEN JU’UMINE MIN KAWMIKE ‘ILLA MEN KAD ‘AMENE FELA TEBTE’IS BIMA KANU JEF’ALUNE
11|37|WE ESNA’IL-FULKE BI’A’JUNINA WE WEHJINA WE LA TUHATIBNI FIL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ‘INNEHUM MUGREKUNE
11|38|WE JESNA’UL-FULKE WE KULLEMA MERRE ‘ALEJHI MELE’UN MIN KAWMIHI SEHIRU MINHU KALE ‘IN TESHARU MINNA FE’INNA NESHARU MINKUM KEMA TESHARUNE
11|39|FESEWFE TA’LEMUNE MEN JE’TIHI ‘ADHABUN JUHZIHI WE JEHILLU ‘ALEJHI ‘ADHABUN MUKIMUN
11|40|HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’E ‘EMRUNA WE FARET-TENNURU KULNA EHMIL FIHA MIN KULLIN ZEWXHEJNI ETHNEJNI WE ‘EHLEKE ‘ILLA MEN SEBEKA ‘ALEJHIL-KAWLU WE MEN ‘AMENE WE MA ‘AMENE ME’AHU ‘ILLA KALILUN
11|41|WE KALE ERKEBU FIHA BISMI ELLAHI MEXHRAHA WE MURSAHA ‘INNE RABBI LEGAFURUN REHIMUN
11|42|WE HIJE TEXHRI BIHIM FI MEWXHIN KALXHIBALI WE NADA NUHUN EBNEHU WE KANE FI MA’ZILIN JA BUNEJJE ERKEB ME’ANA WE LA TEKUN ME’AL-KAFIRINE
11|43|KALE SE’AWI ‘ILA XHEBELIN JA’SIMUNI MINEL-MA’I KALE LA ‘ASIMEL-JEWME MIN ‘EMRI ELLAHI ‘ILLA MEN REHIME WE HALE BEJNEHUMAL-MEWXHU FEKANE MINEL-MUGREKINE
11|44|WE KILE JA ‘ERDU EBLA’I MA’EKI WE JA SEMA’U ‘EKLI’I WE GIDEL-MA’U WE KUDIJEL-’EMRU WE ESTEWET ‘ALEL-XHUDIJI WE KILE BU’DÆN LILKAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
11|45|WE NADA NUHUN REBBEHU FEKALE RABBI ‘INNE EBNI MIN ‘EHLI WE ‘INNE WA’DEKEL-HEKKU WE ‘ENTE ‘EHKEMUL-HAKIMINE
11|46|KALE JA NUHU ‘INNEHU LEJSE MIN ‘EHLIKE ‘INNEHU ‘AMELUN GAJRU SALIHIN FELA TES’ELNI MA LEJSE LEKE BIHI ‘ILMUN ‘INNI ‘A’IDHUKE ‘EN TEKUNE MINEL-XHAHILINE
11|47|KALE RABBI ‘INNI ‘A’UDHU BIKE ‘EN ‘ES’ELEKE MA LEJSE LI BIHI ‘ILMUN WE ‘ILLA TEGFIR LI WE TERHEMNI ‘EKUN MINEL-HASIRINE
11|48|KILE JA NUHU EHBIT BISELAMIN MINNA WE BEREKATIN ‘ALEJKE WE ‘ALA ‘UMEMIN MIMMEN ME’AKE WE ‘UMEMUN SENUMETTI’UHUM THUMME JEMESSUHUM MINNA ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
11|49|TILKE MIN ‘ENBA’IL-GAJBI NUHIHA ‘ILEJKE MA KUNTE TA’LEMUHA ‘ENTE WE LA KAWMUKE MIN KABLI HADHA FASBIR ‘INNEL-’AKIBETE LILMUTTEKINE
11|50|WE ‘ILA ‘ADIN ‘EHAHUM HUDÆN KALE JA KAWMI A’BUDU ELLAHE MA LEKUM MIN ‘ILEHIN GAJRUHU ‘IN ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA MUFTERUNE

11|57|FE’IN TEWELLEW FEKAD ‘EBLEGTUKUM MA ‘URSILTU BIHI ‘ILEJKUM WE JESTEHLIFU RABBI KAWMÆN GAJREKUM WE LA TEDURRUNEHU SHEJ’ÆN ‘INNE RABBI ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN HEFIDHUN

12|18|WE XHA’U ‘ALA KAMISIHI BIDEMIN KEDHIBIN KALE BEL SEWWELET LEKUM ‘ENFUSUKUM ‘EMRÆN FESEBRUN XHEMILUN WEL-LAHUL-MUSTA’ANU ‘ALA MA TESIFUNE
12|19|WE XHA’ET SEJJARETUN FE’ERSELU WE ERIDEHUM FE’EDLA DELWEHU KALE JA BUSHRA HADHA GULAMUN WE ‘ESERRUHU BIDA’ATEN WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN BIMA JA’MELUNE

16|114|FEKULU MIMMA REZEKAKUMU ELLAHU HELALÆN TEJJIBÆN WE ESHKURU NI’METEL-LAHI ‘IN KUNTUM ‘IJAHU TA’BUDUNE
16|115|‘INNEMA HERREME ‘ALEJKUMUL-MEJTETE WE ED-DEME WE LEHMEL-HINZIRI WE MA ‘UHILLE LIGAJRI ELLAHI BIHI FEMENI EDTURRE GAJRE BAGIN WE LA ‘ADIN FE’INNALL-LLAHE GAFURUN REHIMUN
16|116|WE LA TEKULU LIMA TESIFU ‘ELSINETUKUMUL-KEDHIBE HADHA HELALUN WE HEDHA HERAMUN LITEFTERU ‘ALA ELLAHIL-KEDHIBE ‘INNEL-LEDHINE JEFTERUNE ‘ALA ELLAHIL-KEDHIBE LA JUFLIHUNE
16|117|META’UN KALILUN WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
16|118|WE ‘ALEL-LEDHINE HADU HERREMNA MA KASESNA ‘ALEJKE MIN KABLU WE MA DHELEMNAHUM WE LEKIN KANU ‘ENFUSEHUM JEDHLIMUNE
16|119|THUMME ‘INNE REBBEKE LILLEDHINE ‘AMILU ES-SU’E BIXHEHALETIN THUMME TABU MIN BA’DI DHALIKE WE ‘ESLEHU ‘INNE REBBEKE MIN BA’DIHA LEGAFURUN REHIMUN
16|120|‘INNE ‘IBRAHIME KANE ‘UMMETEN KANITÆN LILLAHI HENIFÆN WE LEM JEKU MINEL-MUSHRIKINE
16|121|SHAKIRÆN LI’N’UMIHI EXHTEBAHU WE HEDAHU ‘ILA SIRATIN MUSTEKIM
16|122|WE ‘ATEJNAHU FI ED-DUNJA HESENETEN WE ‘INNEHU FIL-’AHIRETI LEMINE ES-SALIHINE
16|123|THUMME ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE ‘ENI ETTEBI’ MILLETE ‘IBRAHIME HENIFÆN WE MA KANE MINEL-MUSHRIKINE
16|124|‘INNEMA XHU’ILE ES-SEBTU ‘ALEL-LEDHINE EHTELEFU FIHI WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEJEHKUMU BEJNEHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI FIMA KANU FIHI JEHTELIFUNE
16|125|ED’U ‘ILA SEBILI RABBIKE BIL-HIKMETI WEL-MEW’IDHETIL-HESENETI WE XHADILHUM BI-ETI HIJE ‘EHSENU ‘INNE REBBEKE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMEN DELLE ‘AN SEBILIHI WE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIL-MUHTEDINE
16|126|WE ‘IN ‘AKABTUM FA’AKIBU BIMITHLI MA ‘UKIBTUM BIHI WE LE’IN SEBERTUM LEHUWE HAJRUN LILSSABIRINE
16|127|WE ESBIR WE MA SEBRUKE ‘ILLA BILLAHI WE LA TEHZEN ‘ALEJHIM WE LA TEKU FI DEJKIN MIMMA JEMKURUNE
16|128|‘INNALL-LLAHE ME’AL-LEDHINE ETTEKAW WEL-LEDHINE HUM MUHSINUNE
17|1|SUBHANEL-LEDHI ‘ESRA BI’ABDIHI LEJLÆN MINEL-MESXHIDIL-HERAMI ‘ILAL-MESXHIDIL-’EKSAL-LEDHI BAREKNA HEWLEHU LINURIJEHU MIN ‘AJATINA ‘INNEHU HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-BESIRU
17|2|WE ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE WE XHE’ALNAHU HUDEN LIBENI ‘ISRA’ILE ‘ELLA TETTEHIDHU MIN DUNI WE KILÆN
17|3|DHURRIJETE MEN HEMELNA ME’A NUHIN ‘INNEHU KANE ‘ABDÆN SHEKURÆN
17|4|WE KADEJNA ‘ILA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE FIL-KITABI LETUFSIDUNNE FIL-’ERDI MERRETEJNI WE LETA’LUNNE ‘ULUWÆN KEBIRÆN
17|5|FE’IDHA XHA’E WA’DU ‘ULAHUMA BE’ATHNA ‘ALEJKUM ‘IBADÆN LENA ‘ULI BE’SIN SHEDIDIN FEXHASU HILALE ED-DIJARI WE KANE WA’DÆN MEF’ULÆN
17|6|THUMME REDEDNA LEKUMUL-KERRETE ‘ALEJHIM WE ‘EMDEDNAKUM BI’EMWALIN WE BENINE WE XHE’ALNAKUM ‘EKTHERE NEFIRÆN
17|7|‘IN ‘EHSENTUM ‘EHSENTUM LI’NFUSIKUM WE ‘IN ‘ESE’TUM FELEHA FE’IDHA XHA’E WA’DUL-’AHIRETI LIJESU’U WUXHUHEKUM WE LIJEDHULUL-MESXHIDE KEMA DEHALUHU ‘EWWELE MERRETIN WE LIJUTEBBIRU MA ‘ALEW TETBIRÆN
17|8|‘ASA REBBUKUM ‘EN JERHEMEKUM WE ‘IN ‘UDTUM ‘UDNA WE XHE’ALNA XHEHENNEME LILKAFIRINE HESIRÆN
17|9|‘INNE HADHAL-KUR’ANE JEHDI LILLETI HIJE ‘EKWEMU WE JUBESHSHIRUL-MU’UMININEL-LEDHINE JA’MELUNE ES-SALIHATI ‘ENNE LEHUM ‘EXHRÆN KEBIRÆN
17|10|WE ‘ENNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI ‘A’TEDNA LEHUM ‘ADHABÆN ‘ELIMÆN
17|11|WE JED’UL-’INSANU BISH-SHERRI DU’A’EHU BIL-HAJRI WE KANEL-’INSANU ‘AXHULÆN
17|12|WE XHE’ALNAL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE ‘AJETEJNI FEMEHEWNA ‘AJETEL-LEJLI WE XHE’ALNA ‘AJETE EN-NEHARI MUBSIRETEN LITEBTEGU FEDLÆN MIN RABBIKUM WE LITA’LEMU ‘ADEDE ES-SININE WEL-HISABE WE KULLE SHEJ’IN FESSELNAHU TEFSILÆN
17|13|WE KULLE ‘INSANIN ‘ELZEMNAHU TA’IREHU FI ‘UNUKIHI WE NUHRIXHU LEHU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI KITABÆN JELKAHU MENSHURÆN
17|14|EKRE’ KITABEKE KEFA BINEFSIKEL-JEWME ‘ALEJKE HESIBÆN
17|15|MENI EHTEDA FE’INNEMA JEHTEDI LINEFSIHI WE MEN DELLE FE’INNEMA JEDILLU ‘ALEJHA WE LA TEZIRU WAZIRETUN WIZRE ‘UHRA WE MA KUNNA MU’ADHDHIBINE HETTA NEB’ATHE RESULÆN
17|16|WE ‘IDHA ‘EREDNA ‘EN NUHLIKE KARJETEN ‘EMERNA MUTREFIHA FEFESEKU FIHA FEHEKKA ‘ALEJHAL-KAWLU FEDEMMERNAHA TEDMIRÆN
17|17|WE KEM ‘EHLEKNA MINEL-KURUNI MIN BA’DI NUHIN WE KEFA BIREBBIKE BIDHUNUBI ‘IBADIHI HABIRÆN BESIRÆN
17|18|MEN KANE JURIDUL-’AXHILETE ‘AXHXHELNA LEHU FIHA MA NESHA’U LIMEN NURIDU THUMME XHE’ALNA LEHU XHEHENNEME JESLAHA MEDHMUMÆN MEDHURÆN
17|19|WE MEN ‘ERADEL-’AHIRETE WE SA’A LEHA SA’JEHA WE HUWE MU’UMINUN FE’ULA’IKE KANE SA’JUHUM MESHKURÆN
17|20|KULLÆN NUMIDDU HA’UULA’ WE HA’UULA’ MIN ‘ATA’I RABBIKE WE MA KANE ‘ATA’U RABBIKE MEHDHURÆN
17|21|ENDHUR KEJFE FEDDELNA BA’DEHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN WE LEL’AHIRETU ‘EKBERU DEREXHATIN WE ‘EKBERU TEFDILÆN
17|22|LA TEXH’AL ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE FETEK’UDE MEDHMUMÆN MEHDHULÆN
17|23|WE KADA REBBUKE ‘ELLA TA’BUDU ‘ILLA ‘IJAHU WE BIL-WALIDEJNI ‘IHSANÆN ‘IMMA JEBLUGANNE ‘INDEKEL-KIBERE ‘EHEDUHUMA ‘EW KILAHUMA FELA TEKUL LEHUMA ‘UFFIN WE LA TENHERHUMA WE KUL LEHUMA KAWLÆN KERIMÆN
17|24|WE EHFID LEHUMA XHENAHE EDH-DHULLI MINE ER-REHMETI WE KUL RREBBI ERHEMHUMA KEMA REBBEJANI SEGIRÆN

17|34|WE LA TEKREBU MALEL-JETIMI ‘ILLA BI-ETI HIJE ‘EHSENU HETTA JEBLUGA ‘ESHUDDEHU WE ‘EWFU BIL-’AHDI ‘INNEL-’AHDE KANE MES’ULÆN

17|37|WE LA TEMSHI FIL-’ERDI MEREHÆN ‘INNEKE LEN TEHRIKAL-’ERDE WE LEN TEBLUGAL-XHIBALE TULÆN
17|38|KULLU DHALIKE KANE SEJJI’UHU ‘INDE RABBIKE MEKRUHÆN
17|39|DHALIKE MIMMA ‘EWHA ‘ILEJKE REBBUKE MINEL-HIKMETI WE LA TEXH’AL ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE FETULKA FI XHEHENNEME MELUMÆN MEDHURÆN
17|40|‘EFE’ESFAKUM REBBUKUM BIL-BENINE WE ETTEHADHE MINEL-MELA’IKETI ‘INATHÆN ‘INNEKUM LETEKULUNE KAWLÆN ‘ADHIMÆN

17|43|SUBHANEHU WE TA’ALA ‘AMMA JEKULUNE ‘ULUWÆN KEBIRÆN
17|44|TUSEBBIHU LEHU ES-SEMAWATU ES-SEB’U WEL-’ERDU WE MEN FIHINNE WE ‘IN MIN SHEJ’IN ‘ILLA JUSEBBIHU BIHEMDIHI WE LEKIN LA TEFKAHUNE TESBIHEHUM ‘INNEHU KANE HELIMÆN GAFURÆN
17|45|WE ‘IDHA KARE’TEL-KUR’ANE XHE’ALNA BEJNEKE WE BEJNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI HIXHABÆN MESTURÆN

17|78|‘EKIMI ES-SELÆTE LIDULUKI ESH-SHEMSI ‘ILA GASEKIL-LEJLI WE KUR’ANEL-FEXHRI ‘INNE KUR’ANEL-FEXHRI KANE MESH/HUDÆN

17|100|KUL LEW ‘ENTUM TEMLIKUNE HAZA’INE REHMETI RABBI ‘IDHÆN LE’EMSEKTUM HASHJETEL-’INFAKI WE KANEL-’INSANU KATURÆN

17|102|KALE LEKAD ‘ALIMTE MA ‘ENZELE HA’UULA’ ‘ILLA REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI BESA’IRE WE ‘INNI LE’EDHUNNUKE JA FIR’AWNU METHBURÆN
17|103|FE’ERADE ‘EN JESTEFIZZEHUM MINEL-’ERDI FE’EGREKNAHU WE MEN ME’AHU XHEMI’ÆN

17|105|WE BIL-HEKKI ‘ENZELNAHU WE BIL-HEKKI NEZELE WE MA ‘ERSELNAKE ‘ILLA MUBESHSHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN
17|106|WE KUR’ANÆN FEREKNAHU LITEKRE’EHU ‘ALA EN-NASI ‘ALA MUKTHIN WE NEZZELNAHU TENZILÆN
17|107|KUL ‘AMINU BIHI ‘EW LA TU’UMINU ‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME MIN KABLIHI ‘IDHA JUTLA ‘ALEJHIM JEHIRRUNE LIL’EDHKANI SUXHXHEDÆN

25|20|WE MA ‘ERSELNA KABLEKE MINEL-MURSELINE ‘ILLA ‘INNEHUM LEJE’KULUNET-TA’AME WE JEMSHUNE FIL-’ESWAKI WE XHE’ALNA BA’DEKUM LIBA’DIN FITNETEN ‘ETESBIRUNE WE KANE REBBUKE BESIRÆN

32|10|WE KALU ‘E’IDHA DELELNA FIL-’ERDI ‘E’INNA LEFI HALKIN XHEDIDIN BEL HUM BILIKA’I RABBIHIM KAFIRUNE
32|11|KUL JETEWEFFAKUM MELEKUL-MEWTIL-LEDHI WUKKILE BIKUM THUMME ‘ILA RABBIKUM TURXHA’UNE
32|12|WE LEW TERA ‘IDHIL-MUXHRIMUNE NAKISU RU’USIHIM ‘INDE RABBIHIM REBBENA ‘EBSERNA WE SEMI’NA FARXHI’NA NA’MEL SALIHÆN ‘INNA MUKINUNE
32|13|WE LEW SHI’NA LE’ATEJNA KULLE NEFSIN HUDAHA WE LEKIN HEKKAL-KAWLU MINNI LE’EMLE’ENNE XHEHENNEME MINEL-XHINNETI WE EN-NASI ‘EXHMA’INE
32|14|FEDHUKU BIMA NESITUM LIKA’E JEWMIKUM HADHA ‘INNA NESINAKUM WE DHUKU ‘ADHABEL-HULDI BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
32|15|‘INNEMA JU’UMINU BI’AJATINAL-LEDHINE ‘IDHA DHUKKIRU BIHA HARRU SUXHXHEDÆN WE SEBBEHU BIHEMDI RABBIHIM WE HUM LA JESTEKBIRUNE
32|16|TETEXHAFA XHUNUBUHUM ‘ANIL-MEDAXHI’I JED’UNE REBBEHUM HAWFÆN WE TEMA’ÆN WE MIMMA REZEKNAHUM JUNFIKUNE
32|17|FELA TA’LEMU NEFSUN MA ‘UHFIJE LEHUM MIN KURRETI ‘A’JUNIN XHEZA’EN BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
32|18|‘EFEMEN KANE MU’UMINÆN KEMEN KANE FASIKÆN LA JESTEWUNE
32|19|‘EMMAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI FELEHUM XHENNATUL-ME’WA NUZULÆN BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
32|20|WE ‘EMMAL-LEDHINE FESEKU FEME’WAHUMU EN-NARU KULLEMA ‘ERADU ‘EN JEHRUXHU MINHA ‘U’IDU FIHA WE KILE LEHUM DHUKU ‘ADHABE EN-NARIL-LEDHI KUNTUM BIHI TUKEDHDHIBUNE
32|21|WE LENUDHIKANNEHUM MINEL-’ADHABIL-’EDNA DUNEL-’ADHABIL-’EKBERI LE’ALLEHUM JERXHI’UNE

32|24|WE XHE’ALNA MINHUM ‘E’IMMETEN JEHDUNE BI’EMRINA LEMMA SEBERU WE KANU BI’AJATINA JUKINUNE

32|27|‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNA NESUKUL-MA’E ‘ILAL-’ERDIL-XHURUZI FENUHRIXHU BIHI ZER’ÆN TE’KULU MINHU ‘EN’AMUHUM WE ‘ENFUSUHUM ‘EFELA JUBSIRUNE
32|28|WE JEKULUNE META HADHAL-FETHU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
32|29|KUL JEWMEL-FETHI LA JENFA’UL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘IMANUHUM WE LA HUM JUNDHERUNE
32|30|FE’A’RID ‘ANHUM WE ENTEDHIR ‘INNEHUM MUNTEDHIRUNE
33|1|JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU ETTEKI ELLAHE WE LA TUTI’IL-KAFIRINE WEL-MUNAFIKINE ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE ‘ALIMÆN HEKIMÆN
33|2|WE ETTEBI’ MA JUHA ‘ILEJKE MIN RABBIKE ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE BIMA TA’MELUNE HABIRÆN
33|3|WE TEWEKKEL ‘ALA ELLAHI WE KEFA BILLAHI WE KILÆN
33|4|MA XHE’ALEL-LAHU LIREXHULIN MIN KALBEJNI FI XHEWFIHI WE MA XHE’ALE ‘EZWAXHEKUMUL-LA’I TUDHAHIRUNE MINHUNNE ‘UMMEHATIKUM WE MA XHE’ALE ‘ED’IJA’EKUM ‘EBNA’EKUM DHALIKUM KAWLUKUM BI’EFWAHIKUM WEL-LAHU JEKULUL-HEKKA WE HUWE JEHDI ES-SEBILE
33|5|ED’UHUM LI’EBA’IHIM HUWE ‘EKSETU ‘INDEL-LAHI FE’IN LEM TA’LEMU ‘ABA’EHUM FE’IHWANUKUM FI ED-DINI WE MEWALIKUM WE LEJSE ‘ALEJKUM XHUNAHUN FIMA ‘EHTE’TUM BIHI WE LEKIN MA TE’AMMEDET KULUBUKUM WE KANEL-LAHU GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
33|6|EN-NEBIJU ‘EWLA BIL-MU’UMININE MIN ‘ENFUSIHIM WE ‘EZWAXHUHU ‘UMMEHATUHUM WE ‘ULUL-’ERHAMI BA’DUHUM ‘EWLA BIBA’DIN FI KITABI ELLAHI MINEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MUHAXHIRINE ‘ILLA ‘EN TEF’ALU ‘ILA ‘EWLIJA’IKUM MA’RUFÆN KANE DHALIKE FIL-KITABI MESTURÆN

33|10|‘IDH XHA’UKUM MIN FEWKIKUM WE MIN ‘ESFELE MINKUM WE ‘IDH ZAGATIL-’EBSARU WE BELEGATIL-KULUBUL-HENAXHIRE WE TEDHUNNUNE BILLAHI EDH-DHUNUNE

33|13|WE ‘IDH KALET TA’IFETUN MINHUM JA ‘EHLE JETHRIBE LA MUKAME LEKUM FARXHI’U WE JESTE’DHINU FERIKUN MINHUMU EN-NEBIJE JEKULUNE ‘INNE BUJUTENA ‘AWRETUN WE MA HIJE BI’AWRETIN ‘IN JURIDUNE ‘ILLA FIRARÆN
33|14|WE LEW DUHILET ‘ALEJHIM MIN ‘EKTARIHA THUMME SU’ILUL-FITNETE LE’ATEWHA WE MA TELEBBETHU BIHA ‘ILLA JESIRÆN

33|17|KUL MEN DHAL-LEDHI JA’SIMUKUM MINEL-LAHI ‘IN ‘ERADE BIKUM SU’ÆN ‘EW ‘ERADE BIKUM REHMETEN WE LA JEXHIDUNE LEHUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI WELIJÆN WE LA NESIRÆN
33|18|KAD JA’LEMU ELLAHUL-MU’AWWIKINE MINKUM WEL-KA’ILINE LI’IHWANIHIM HELUMME ‘ILEJNA WE LA JE’TUNEL-BE’SE ‘ILLA KALILÆN
33|19|‘ESHIHHETEN ‘ALEJKUM FE’IDHA XHA’EL-HAWFU RE’EJTEHUM JENDHURUNE ‘ILEJKE TEDURU ‘A’JUNUHUM KALLEDHI JUGSHA ‘ALEJHI MINEL-MEWTI FE’IDHA DHEHEBEL-HAWFU SELEKUKUM BI’ELSINETIN HIDADIN ‘ESHIHHETEN ‘ALEL-HAJRI ‘ULA’IKE LEM JU’UMINU FE’EHBETEL-LAHU ‘A’MALEHUM WE
33|20|JEHSEBUNEL-’EHZABE LEM JEDH/HEBU WE ‘IN JE’TIL-’EHZABU JEWEDDU LEW ‘ENNEHUM BADUNE FIL-’A’RABI JES’ELUNE ‘AN ‘ENBA’IKUM WE LEW KANU FIKUM MA KATELU ‘ILLA KALILÆN
33|21|LEKAD KANE LEKUM FI RESULI ELLAHI ‘USWETUN HESENETUN LIMEN KANE JERXHU ELLAHE WEL-JEWMEL-’AHIRE WE DHEKEREL-LAHE KETHIRÆN
33|22|WE LEMMA RE’AL-MU’UMINUNEL-’EHZABE KALU HADHA MA WE’ADENALLAHU WE RESULUHU WE SEDEKAL-LAHU WE RESULUHU WE MA ZADEHUM ‘ILLA ‘IMANÆN WE TESLIMÆN
33|23|MINEL-MU’UMININE RIXHALUN SEDEKU MA ‘AHEDU ELLAHE ‘ALEJHI FEMINHUM MEN KADA NEHBEHU WE MINHUM MEN JENTEDHIRU WE MA BEDDELU TEBDILÆN
33|24|LIJEXHZIJEL-LAHU ES-SADIKINE BISIDKIHIM WE JU’ADHDHIBEL-MUNAFIKINE ‘IN SHA’E ‘EW JETUBE ‘ALEJHIM ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
33|25|WEREDDEL-LAHUL-LEDHINE KEFERU BIGAJDHIHIM LEM JENALU HAJRÆN WE KEFALLAHUL-MU’UMININEL-KITALE WE KANEL-LAHU KAWIJÆN ‘AZIZÆN
33|26|WE ‘ENZELEL-LEDHINE DHAHERUHUM MIN ‘EHLIL-KITABI MIN SEJASIHIM WE KADHEFE FI KULUBIHIMU ER-RU’BE FERIKÆN TEKTULUNE WE TE’SIRUNE FERIKÆN
33|27|WE ‘EWRETHEKUM ‘ERDEHUM WE DIJAREHUM WE ‘EMWALEHUM WE ‘ERDÆN LEM TETE’UHA WE KANEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRÆN

33|29|WE ‘IN KUNTUNNE TURIDNEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU WE ED-DAREL-’AHIRETE FE’INNALL-LLAHE ‘E’ADDE LILMUHSINATI MINKUNNE ‘EXHRÆN ‘ADHIMÆN

33|31|WE MEN JEKNUT MINKUNNE LILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE TA’MEL SALIHÆN NU’UTIHA ‘EXHREHA MERRETEJNI WE ‘A’TEDNA LEHA RIZKÆN KERIMÆN
33|32|JA NISA’E EN-NEBIJI LESTUNNE KE’EHEDIN MINE EN-NISA’ ‘INI ETTEKAJTUNNE FELA TEHDA’NE BIL-KAWLI FEJETME’AL-LEDHI FI KALBIHI MEREDUN WE KULNE KAWLÆN MA’RUFÆN

33|50|JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU ‘INNA ‘EHLELNA LEKE ‘EZWAXHEKEL-LATI ‘ATEJTE ‘UXHUREHUNNE WE MA MELEKET JEMINUKE MIMMA ‘EFA’EL-LAHU ‘ALEJKE WE BENATI ‘AMMIKE WE BENATI ‘AMMATIKE WE BENATI HALIKE WE BENATI HALATIKEL-LATI HAXHERNE ME’AKE WE EMRE’ETEN MU’UMINETEN ‘IN W

33|58|WEL-LEDHINE JU’UDHUNEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI BIGAJRI MA EKTESEBU FEKADI EHTEMELU BUHTANÆN WE ‘ITHMÆN MUBINÆN

33|60|LE’IN LEM JENTEHIL-MUNAFIKUNE WEL-LEDHINE FI KULUBIHIM MEREDUN WEL-MURXHIFUNE FIL-MEDINETI LENUGRIJENNEKE BIHIM THUMME LA JUXHAWIRUNEKE FIHA ‘ILLA KALILÆN
33|61|MEL’UNINE ‘EJNEMA THUKIFU ‘UHIDHU WE KUTTILU TEKTILÆN
33|62|SUNNETEL-LAHI FIL-LEDHINE HALEW MIN KABLU WE LEN TEXHIDE LISUNNETI ELLAHI TEBDILÆN

33|70|JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ETTEKU ELLAHE WE KULU KAWLÆN SEDIDÆN
33|71|JUSLIH LEKUM ‘A’MALEKUM WE JEGFIR LEKUM DHUNUBEKUM WE MEN JUTI’I ELLAHE WE RESULEHU FEKAD FAZE FEWZÆN ‘ADHIMÆN
33|72|‘INNA ‘AREDNAL-’EMANETE ‘ALA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WEL-XHIBALI FE’EBEJNE ‘EN JEHMILNEHA WE ‘ESHFEKNE MINHA WE HEMELEHAL-’INSANU ‘INNEHU KANE DHELUMÆN XHEHULÆN
33|73|LIJU’ADHDHIBEL-LAHUL-MUNAFIKINE WEL-MUNAFIKATI WEL-MUSHRIKINE WEL-MUSHRIKATI WE JETUBEL-LAHU ‘ALEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI WE KANEL-LAHU GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
34|1|EL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE LEHUL-HEMDU FIL-’AHIRETI WE HUWEL-HEKIMUL-HABIRU
34|2|JA’LEMU MA JELIXHU FIL-’ERDI WE MA JEHRUXHU MINHA WE MA JENZILU MINE ES-SEMA’I WE MA JA’RUXHU FIHA WE HUWE ER-REHIMUL-GAFURU
34|3|WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LA TE’TINA ES-SA’ATU KUL BELA WE RABBI LETE’TIJENNEKUM ‘ALIMIL-GAJBI LA JA’ZUBU ‘ANHU MITHKALU DHERRETIN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE LA FIL-’ERDI WE LA ‘ESGARU MIN DHALIKE WE LA ‘EKBERU ‘ILLA FI KITABIN MUBININ
34|4|LIJEXHZIJEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM MEGFIRETUN WE RIZKUN KERIMUN
34|5|WEL-LEDHINE SE’AW FI ‘AJATINA MU’AXHIZINE ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN MIN RIXHZIN ‘ELIMUN
34|6|WE JERAL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILMEL-LEDHI ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJKE MIN RABBIKE HUWEL-HEKKA WE JEHDI ‘ILA SIRATIL-’AZIZIL-HEMIDI
34|7|WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU HEL NEDULLUKUM ‘ALA REXHULIN JUNEBBI’UKUM ‘IDHA MUZZIKTUM KULLE MUMEZZEKIN ‘INNEKUM LEFI HALKIN XHEDIDIN
34|8|‘AFTERA ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN ‘EM BIHI XHINNETUN BELIL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI FIL-’ADHABI WE ED-DELALIL-BA’IDI
34|9|‘EFELEM JEREW ‘ILA MA BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE MA HALFEHUM MINE ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI ‘IN NESHE’ NEHSIF BIHIMUL-’ERDE ‘EW NUSKIT ‘ALEJHIM KISEFÆN MINE ES-SEMA’I ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKULLI ‘ABDIN MUNIBIN
34|10|WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA DAWUDE MINNA FEDLÆN JA XHIBALU ‘EWWIBI ME’AHU WET-TEJRE WE ‘ELENNA LEHUL-HEDIDE
34|11|‘ENI A’MEL SABIGATIN WE KADDIR FI ES-SERDI WE A’MELU SALIHÆN ‘INNI BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRUN
34|12|WE LISULEJMANE ER-RIHE GUDUWUHA SHEHRUN WE REWAHUHA SHEHRUN WE ‘ESELNA LEHU ‘AJNEL-KITRI WE MINEL-XHINNI MEN JA’MELU BEJNE JEDEJHI BI’IDHNI RABBIHI WE MEN JEZIG MINHUM ‘AN ‘EMRINA NUDHIKHU MIN ‘ADHABI ES-SA’IRI
34|13|JA’MELUNE LEHU MA JESHA’U MIN MEHARIBE WE TEMATHILE WE XHIFANIN KALXHEWABI WE KUDURIN RASIJATIN A’MELU ‘ALE DAWUDE SHUKRÆN WE KALILUN MIN ‘IBADIJE ESH-SHEKURU
34|14|FELEMMA KADEJNA ‘ALEJHIL-MEWTE MA DELLEHUM ‘ALA MEWTIHI ‘ILLA DABBETUL-’ERDI TE’KULU MINSE’ETEHU FELEMMA HARRE TEBEJJENETIL-XHINNU ‘EN LEW KANU JA’LEMUNEL-GAJBE MA LEBITHU FIL-’ADHABIL-MUHINI
34|15|LEKAD KANE LISEBE’IIN FI MESKENIHIM ‘AJETUN XHENNETANI ‘AN JEMININ WE SHIMALIN KULU MIN RIZKI RABBIKUM WE ESHKURU LEHU BELDETUN TEJJIBETUN WE REBBUN GAFURUN
34|16|FE’A’REDU FE’ERSELNA ‘ALEJHIM SEJLEL-’ARIMI WE BEDDELNAHUM BIXHENNETEJHIM XHENNETEJNI DHEWATA ‘UKULIN HAMTIN WE ‘ETHLIN WE SHEJ’IN MIN SIDRIN KALILIN
34|17|DHALIKE XHEZEJNAHUM BIMA KEFERU WE HEL NUXHAZI ‘ILLAL-KEFURE
34|18|WE XHE’ALNA BEJNEHUM WE BEJNEL-KURA ELLETI BAREKNA FIHA KUREN DHAHIRETEN WE KADDERNA FIHA ES-SEJRE SIRU FIHA LEJALIJE WE ‘EJJAMÆN ‘AMININE
34|19|FEKALU REBBENA BA’ID BEJNE ‘ESFARINA WE DHELEMU ‘ENFUSEHUM FEXHE’ALNAHUM ‘EHADITHE WE MEZZEKNAHUM KULLE MUMEZZEKIN ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKULLI SEBBARIN SHEKURIN
34|20|WE LEKAD SEDDEKA ‘ALEJHIM ‘IBLISU DHENNEHU FE ETTEBA’UHU ‘ILLA FERIKÆN MINEL-MU’UMININE
34|21|WE MA KANE LEHU ‘ALEJHIM MIN SULTANIN ‘ILLA LINA’LEME MEN JU’UMINU BIL-’AHIRETI MIMMEN HUWE MINHA FI SHEKKIN WE REBBUKE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN HEFIDHUN
34|22|KUL ED’UL-LEDHINE ZE’AMTUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI LA JEMLIKUNE MITHKALE DHERRETIN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE LA FIL-’ERDI WE MA LEHUM FIHIMA MIN SHIRKIN WE MA LEHU MINHUM MIN DHEHIRIN
34|23|WE LA TENFA’U ESH-SHEFA’ATU ‘INDEHU ‘ILLA LIMEN ‘EDHINE LEHU HETTA ‘IDHA FUZZI’A ‘AN KULUBIHIM KALU MADHA KALE REBBUKUM KALUL-HEKKA WE HUWEL-’ALIJUL-KEBIRU
34|24|KUL MEN JERZUKUKUM MINE ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI KULI ELLAHU WE ‘INNA ‘EW ‘IJAKUM LE’ALA HUDEN ‘EW FI DELALIN MUBININ

34|30|KUL LEKUM MI’ADU JEWMIN LA TESTE’HIRUNE ‘ANHU SA’ATEN WE LA TESTEKDIMUNE
34|31|WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEN NU’UMINE BIHEDHAL-KUR’ANI WE LA BIEL-LEDHI BEJNE JEDEJHI WE LEW TERA ‘IDHI EDH-DHALIMUNE MEWKUFUNE ‘INDE RABBIHIM JERXHI’U BA’DUHUM ‘ILA BA’DINL-KAWLE JEKULUL-LEDHINE ESTUD’IFU LILLEDHINE ESTEKBERU LEWLA ‘ENTUM LEKUNNA MU’UMINI

34|33|WE KALEL-LEDHINE ESTUD’IFU LILLEDHINE ESTEKBERU BEL MEKRUL-LEJLI WE EN-NEHARI ‘IDH TE’MURUNENA ‘EN NEKFURE BILLAHI WE NEXH’ALE LEHU ‘ENDADÆN WE ‘ESERRU EN-NEDAMETE LEMMA RE’EWL-’ADHABE WE XHE’ALNAL-’EGLALE FI ‘A’NAKIL-LEDHINE KEFERU HEL JUXHZEWNE ‘ILLA MA

34|37|WE MA ‘EMWALUKUM WE LA ‘EWLADUKUM BI-ETI TUKARRIBUKUM ‘INDENA ZULFA ‘ILLA MEN ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FE’ULA’IKE LEHUM XHEZA’U ED-DI’FI BIMA ‘AMILU WE HUM FIL-GURUFATI ‘AMINUNE

35|1|EL-HEMDU LILLAHI FATIRI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI XHA’ILIL-MELA’IKETI RUSULÆN ‘ULI ‘EXHNIHETIN METHNA WE THULATHE WE RUBA’A JEZIDU FIL-HALKI MA JESHA’U ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN

38|25|FEGAFERNA LEHU DHALIKE WE ‘INNE LEHU ‘INDENA LEZULFA WE HUSNE ME’ABIN

38|27|WE MA HALEKNA ES-SEMA’E WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA BATILÆN DHALIKE DHENNUL-LEDHINE KEFERU FEWEJLUN LILLEDHINE KEFERU MINE EN-NARI
38|28|‘EM NEXH’ALUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI KALMUFSIDINE FIL-’ERDI ‘EM NEXH’ALUL-MUTTEKINE KALFUXHXHARI

38|36|FESEHHARNA LEHU ER-RIHE TEXHRI BI’EMRIHI RUHA’EN HEJTHU ‘ESABE
